5589<h2 style="text-align: center;">

5590&nbsp;</h2>

5593<p>

Because of our unique relationship to high-quality brands and manufacturers, we are poised to provide you the best deals and products for your home improvement needs.</p>

5648<h2 dir="ltr" style="text-align: center;">

5649Our Unique Pricing</h2>

5650

5651

5652<h2 dir="ltr" style="text-align: center;">

5653&nbsp;</h2>

5654

5655

5656<p>

5657Our goal is to provide both expert interior design for your space and source the best products for your vision. While most home interior designers charge by the hour, we charge a modest, flat fee. We deduct this retainer fee from any products you purchase through a Vevano designer so that all of your budget can go towards the products and installation that will achieve your dream design.</p>
